The \"Cards\" is on the left-hand side of the app to reference a list of customers, inventory items and pricing. This is a metaphor that most of us, who need to issue invoices, can understand, visualize and associate with. We gleaned this metaphor from previous experiences where we successfully helped fast-growing companies transform their on the go manual \"Cards-and-Paper\" invoice issuance to that of a fully automated one using our software.
